 4
 a trial run on the 295-km-long dwarka-najafgarh metro corridor took place on Monday
 is coridor main dwarka, nangali or najafagarh teen stesan shaamil hai, isamen dwarka or nangali alivated stesan hai, jabaki najafagarh underground (bhumigat) stesan he
 Delhi Metro Rail Corporation (DMRC) has given color code of gray line to this entire line
 metro kii grey line ko sitambar, 2019 tak puraa karne kaa target rakhaa gaya he
 1 to this section
 18 kilometre aage dhansa stand tak badhaayaa jayega, jise disambar 2020 tak puraa kiya janaa he

 tippaniyan a laddu of 7,000 kg is being prepared for the Vinayaka Chaturthi Festival organized by the Rajahmundry Ganesh Utsav Committee (RGUC) at Pushkar Ghat in Rajahmundry in East Godavari district in Andhra Pradesh
 do baar ginis ricard main apana naam darj karvaa chuke jile ke tapeshwaram ke shri bhaktanjaneya sweets ke maalik es venkateshwar raav ne bataaya ki arjiusi dwaara aadesh die jane ke baad ham log 7,000 kilogram kaa ek laddu bana rahe hai
 It will be handed over to managers at 10 am on Monday

 Although laptops, smartphones and tablet pcs are used extensively nowadays, but when it comes to knowing the news of the country and the world, most people gaze at the 'idiot box' ie TV
 ji haa, ‘bibisi world news’ ke liye ‘incits kansalting’ dwaara kiye gaye ek adhyayan ke nattejey to yahi bayaan karte hai
 Those included in the study said that they spend 42 per cent of their time on television while 29 per cent of their time is spent on laptops
 smart phone par 18 fisadi jabaki tablet pisi par mahaj 10 fisadi vakt khabaren dekhne main kharch karte hai log
 According to the study of 'insights Consulting', these different ways of knowing the news are not being complementary to each other, but like a supplement
 tippaniyan BBC Global News CEO Jim Egan said, "for many years, there was speculation that the increase in the use of smart phones, laptops and tablet pcs would cause TV viewership to decline
 lekin is adhyayan se pataa chalaa he ki chaaron upkaran ekasaath behatar kaam kar rahe hai, jisase har kisi ko phayda ho rahaa he
 '' adhyayan ke mutabik, kaamkaaji vakt main smart phone, laptop or tablet pisi kaa zyada istemaal hota he jabaki jaise-jaise shaam dhalati he tivi kaa istemaal bhi badhane lagata he
 During primetime, it is used up to 50 per cent more than other mediums
 ’’ Yes, this is what the results of a study conducted by Insights Consulting for BBC World News say
 adhyayan main shaamil kiye gaye logon ne bataaya ki khabaren dekhne ke liye istemaal kiye gaye vakt main ve 42 fisadi samay tivi ko hi dete hai jabaki 29 fisadi vakt laptop par bitaate hai
 People spend 18% on smart phones while only 10% of the time spent watching news on tablet pcs
 ‘incits kansalting’ ke adhyayan kii maane to khabaren jaanane ke ye alag-alag jariye ek-duusare ke pratidwandi nahin balki poorak kii tarah pesh aa rahe hai
 The comments ‘bibisi global news’ ke siio gym eagan ne bataaya, ‘‘kai saal se aisi atakalein thim ki smart phone, laptop or tablet pisi ke istemaal main ijaphe se tivi ko darshakon kii kami hogi
 But this study showed that all four devices are working better together, benefiting everyone
 ’’ According to the study, smart phones, laptops and tablet pcs are used more during working hours, while the usage of TV also starts to increase as the evening progresses
 primetime ke vakt to iskaa istemaal duusare madhyamon se 50 fisadi adhik tak hota he

 ’’ Samajwadi Party, which is looking for opportunities in Madhya Pradesh and Chhattisgarh, has got a new partner before the Vidhan Sabha elections

 On Sunday (21 October) GGP Chief Heera Singh Markam made this announcement

 Due to continuous delays in the alliance, the party has now decided to contest elections with Akhilesh Yadav
 jijipi mukhiya hira singh ne kaha ki congress gathbandhan main deree kar rahi he or ab chhattisgarh main namakan kii bhi prakriya shuru ho gai he, isliye unke saath ab chunaav main utarana sambhav nahin he
 The Gondwana Ganatantra Party will now contest 60 seats in Chhattisgarh, while the Samajwadi Party has got 18 seats
 samaajawaadee party ke chunaav chihn cycle kaa zikr karte hue unhone kaha ki 'handle hamaare haath main he, jabaki pedal unke niyantran main he
 "let us know that GGP has a good reach in tribal dominated areas of Chhattisgarh and Madhya Pradesh
 congress ke saath gathbandhan fail hone par unhone bataaya ki congress ke kuch netaa jijipi netaaon se baat karte hai, lekin ve kabhi bhi jimmedaar aadmi ke paas apni baat nahin rakhte hai

 or yadi baat bhi karata he to kahata he ki ek seat le lo, teen seat le lo
